                Coronavirus song: Filipinos outraged over Chinese embassy’s South China Sea ‘propaganda video’
            </h1><div class="info__subHeadline" data-v-0ff1f739><div data-v-0ff1f739><ul class="generic-article__summary--ul content--ul" data-v-e4bae94c data-v-0ff1f739>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-e4bae94c>The Chinese embassy in Manila says it is a friendship song dedicated to health workers from both countries</li>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-e4bae94c>But Filipino netizens say the music video’s imagery of a sea shared by China and the Philippines amounts to ‘propaganda’</li>
